behavior load_washing_machine(clothes:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(clothes, washing_machine)
        # Load the clothes into the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve is_on(washing_machine)
        # Turn on the washing machine to start washing

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket for clothes

        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Select the washing machine

        foreach c: item:
            if is_clothes(c) and inside(c, basket):
                load_washing_machine(c, washing_machine)
                # Load each piece of clothing from the basket into the washing machine

        start_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Start washing the clothes in the washing machine

#goal_representation_end

#goal_representation

behavior load_clothes(c:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(c, washing_machine)
        # Put the clothes inside the washing machine

behavior close_machine_door(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once closed(washing_machine)
        # Close the washing machine door

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once has_water(washing_machine)
        # Ensure that the washing machine has water to start washing clothes

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket for clothes

        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Select the washing machine

        foreach c: item:
        # Load all clothes from the basket into the washing machine
            if is_clothes(c) and inside(c, basket):
                load_clothes(c, washing_machine)

        close_machine_door(washing_machine) 
        start_washing_machine(washing_machine) 

#goal_representation_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior load_washing_machine(c:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(c, washing_machine)
        # Place the clothing item inside the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once closed(washing_machine) # Close the washing machine door
        achieve_once is_on(washing_machine) # Start the washing machine

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket for clothes

        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine) and id[washing_machine]==2041
        # Select the washing machine with ID 2041

        foreach c: item:
        # Load all clothes from the basket into the washing machine
            if is_clothes(c) and inside(c, basket):
                load_washing_machine(c, washing_machine)
        start_washing_machine(washing_machine) # Start the washing machine

#goal_representation_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior load_washing_machine(clothes:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(clothes, washing_machine)
        # Load the clothes into the washing machine

behavior close_and_turn_on_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once closed(washing_machine) # Close the washing machine door
        achieve_once is_on(washing_machine)  # Turn on the washing machine

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket for clothes
        
        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine) and id[washing_machine]==2041
        # Select the washing machine with ID 2041
        
        foreach clothes: item:
            if is_clothes(clothes) and dirty(clothes) and inside(clothes, basket):
                load_washing_machine(clothes, washing_machine)
        close_and_turn_on_washing_machine(washing_machine)

#goal_representation_end

behavior load_washing_machine(c: item, machine: item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(c, machine)
        # Load the clothes inside the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once closed(machine) # Close the washing machine door
        achieve_once is_on(machine) # Ensure the washing machine is on

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the clothes basket

        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine) and id[washing_machine]==2041
        # Select the washing machine with ID 2041

        foreach c: item:
        # Load all clothes from the basket into the washing machine
            if is_clothes(c) and inside(c, basket):
                load_washing_machine(c, washing_machine)

        start_washing_machine(washing_machine) # Start the washing machine

#goal_representation
 
behavior load_in_washing_machine(clothes:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(clothes, washing_machine)
        # Load clothes into the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once closed(washing_machine) # Close the washing machine door
        achieve_once is_on(washing_machine) # Turn on the washing machine

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket for clothes

        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Select the washing machine

        foreach clothes: item:
        # Load all clothes from the basket into the washing machine
            if is_clothes(clothes) and inside(clothes, basket):
                load_in_washing_machine(clothes, washing_machine)

        start_washing_machine(washing_machine) # Start the washing machine

#goal_representation_end

Goal representation from planning.py

#goal_representation

behavior put_clothes_in_washing_machine(c:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(c, washing_machine)
        # Place the clothing item inside the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once closed(washing_machine) # Close the washing machine door
        achieve is_on(washing_machine) # Ensure the washing machine is on

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket for clothes
        
        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Select the washing machine

        foreach c: item:
        # Load all clothes from the basket into the washing machine
            if is_clothes(c) and inside(c, basket):
                put_clothes_in_washing_machine(c, washing_machine)
                
        start_washing_machine(washing_machine) # Start the washing machine

#goal_representation_end

behavior load_washing_machine(c:item, washing_machine: item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(c, washing_machine)
        # Place the clothes item inside the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine: item):
    body:
        achieve_once is_on(washing_machine) 
        # Turn on the washing machine

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket for clothes

        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Select the washing machine 

        foreach c: item:
            if is_clothes(c) and inside(c, basket):
                load_washing_machine(c, washing_machine)
                # Load all clothes from the basket into the washing machine

        start_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Start the washing machine to wash the clothes

#goal_representation_end

#goal_representation

behavior load_washing_machine(clothes:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(clothes, washing_machine)
        # Load the clothing item into the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once is_on(washing_machine)
        # Start the washing machine

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket for clothes

        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine) and plugged(washing_machine) and is_on(washing_machine)
        # The washing machine should be plugged in and switched on before processing

        foreach clothes: item:
            # Load all clothes from the basket into the washing machine
            if is_clothes(clothes) and inside(clothes, basket):
                load_washing_machine(clothes, washing_machine)

        start_washing_machine(washing_machine) # Start the washing process

#goal_representation_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior load_clothes_into_washing_machine(clothes:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(clothes, washing_machine)
        # Place each clothing item inside the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once closed(washing_machine) # Ensure the washing machine door is closed
        achieve_once is_on(washing_machine) # Switch on the washing machine

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket containing clothes

        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Select a washing machine

        foreach clothes: item:
            if is_clothes(clothes) and dirty(clothes) and inside(clothes, basket):
                load_clothes_into_washing_machine(clothes, washing_machine)
        start_washing_machine(washing_machine) # Start the washing machine to wash the clothes

#goal_representation_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior load_washing_machine(clothes:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(clothes, washing_machine)
        # Load the clothes into the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once closed(washing_machine) # Close the washing machine door
        achieve_once is_on(washing_machine) # Start the washing machine

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket for clothes
        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Select the washing machine
        foreach clothes: item:
            if is_clothes(clothes) and inside(clothes, basket):
                load_washing_machine(clothes, washing_machine)
        start_washing_machine(washing_machine) # Start the washing machine after loading all clothes

#goal_representation_end

behavior load_clothes_into_washing_machine(clothes:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(clothes, washing_machine)
        # Place the clothes into the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once is_on(washing_machine)
        # Turn on the washing machine

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket for clothes

        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine) and id[washing_machine]==2041
        # Select the washing machine with ID 2041

        foreach clothes: item:
        # Load all clothes from the basket into the washing machine
            if is_clothes(clothes) and inside(clothes, basket):
                load_clothes_into_washing_machine(clothes, washing_machine)
        
        start_washing_machine(washing_machine) # Start the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve is_on(washing_machine)
        # Ensure the washing machine remains on to complete the task

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket for clothes
        
        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Select the washing machine

        foreach c: item:
            if is_clothes(c) and inside(c, basket):
                load_washing_machine(c, washing_machine)
                # Load all clothes from the basket into the washing machine

        start_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Start the washing machine

#goal_representation
 
behavior load_washing_machine(c:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(c, washing_machine)
        # Put the clothes inside the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve is_on(washing_machine)
        # Ensure the washing machine is on

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket for clothes
        
        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Select the washing machine
        
        foreach c: item:
            if is_clothes(c) and inside(c, basket):
                load_washing_machine(c, washing_machine)
                # Load each piece of clothing inside the basket to the washing machine
        
        start_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Start the washing machine

#goal_representation_end

behavior load_clothes_into_washing_machine(clothes:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(clothes, washing_machine)
        # Place the clothes inside the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once is_on(washing_machine)
        # Turn on the washing machine

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select a basket for clothes
        
        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Select a washing machine

        foreach clothes: item:
        # Load all clothes from the basket into the washing machine
            if is_clothes(clothes) and inside(clothes, basket):
                load_clothes_into_washing_machine(clothes, washing_machine)
        
        start_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Start the washing machine

#goal_representation
 
behavior load_washing_machine(c:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(c, washing_machine)
        # Place the clothing item inside the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once is_on(washing_machine)
        # Turn on the washing machine to start the wash cycle

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket for clothes
        
        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Select a washing machine

        foreach c: item:
        # Load all clothes from the basket into the washing machine
            if is_clothes(c) and inside(c, basket):
                load_washing_machine(c, washing_machine)
        
        start_washing_machine(washing_machine) # Start the washing machine

#goal_representation_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior load_clothes_from_basket(clothes:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(clothes, washing_machine)

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once closed(washing_machine) # Close the washing machine door
        achieve_once is_on(washing_machine) # Start the washing machine

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket for clothes
        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Select the washing machine
        foreach clothes: item:
        # Load all clothes from the basket into the washing machine
            if is_clothes(clothes) and inside(clothes, basket):
                load_clothes_from_basket(clothes, washing_machine)
        # Start the washing machine
        start_washing_machine(washing_machine)
 
#goal_representation_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior load_clothes_into_washing_machine(clothes:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(clothes, washing_machine)
        # Load the clothes from the basket into the washing machine

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket for clothes
        
        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Select the washing machine

        foreach clothes: item:
        # Load all clothes from the basket into the washing machine
            if is_clothes(clothes) and inside(clothes, basket):
                load_clothes_into_washing_machine(clothes, washing_machine)

        achieve is_on(washing_machine)
        # Ensure the washing machine is turned on

#goal_representation_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior load_clothes_into_washing_machine(c:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(c, washing_machine)
        # Put the item inside the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once closed(washing_machine) # Close the washing machine door
        achieve_once is_on(washing_machine) # Turn on the washing machine

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        foreach c: item:
            if is_clothes(c) and inside(c, basket):
                load_clothes_into_washing_machine(c, washing_machine)
        start_washing_machine(washing_machine)

#goal_representation_end

behavior activate_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):

    body:
        achieve_once inside(c, machine)
        # Ensure clothes are placed inside the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(machine:item):
    body:
        achieve is_on(machine) # Ensure that the washing machine is on

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket containing clothes

        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Select the washing machine

        foreach c: item:
            if is_clothes(c) and inside(c, basket):
                load_clothes_into_washing_machine(c, washing_machine)
        # Load all clothes from the basket into the washing machine

        start_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Start the washing machine

#goal_representation

behavior load_washing_machine(c:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(c, washing_machine)
        # Place each clothing item inside the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once closed(washing_machine) # Close the washing machine door
        achieve is_on(washing_machine) # Turn on the washing machine

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket for clothes

        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Select a washing machine

        foreach c: item:
        # Load all clothes from the basket into the washing machine
            if is_clothes(c) and inside(c, basket):
                load_washing_machine(c, washing_machine)

        start_washing_machine(washing_machine) # Start the washing machine

#goal_representation_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior load_clothes_into_machine(clothes:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(clothes, washing_machine)
        # Place the piece of clothing inside the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once closed(washing_machine) # Close the washing machine door
        achieve is_on(washing_machine) # Turn on the washing machine

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket for clothes
        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Select a washing machine
        foreach clothes: item:
        # Load all clothes from the basket into the washing machine
            if is_clothes(clothes) and inside(clothes, basket):
                load_clothes_into_machine(clothes, washing_machine)
        start_washing_machine(washing_machine) # Start the washing machine

behavior load_washing_machine(c: item, machine: item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(c, machine)
        # Put the clothing item inside the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(machine: item):
    body:
        achieve_once closed(machine)
        # Close the washing machine door
        achieve is_on(machine)
        # Turn on the washing machine

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket for clothes
        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine) and plugged(washing_machine) and is_on(washing_machine)
        # Assume the washing machine is already plugged in and turned on
        foreach c: item:
            if is_clothes(c) and inside(c, basket):
                load_washing_machine(c, washing_machine)
        start_washing_machine(washing_machine)

#goal_representation
 
def has_clothes_in_basket(basket:item):
    # Function to check if there are clothes in the specified basket
    symbol has_clothes = exists o: item : (is_clothes(o) and inside(o, basket))
    return has_clothes

behavior load_washing_machine(clothes:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(clothes, washing_machine)
        # Load the clothes into the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once closed(washing_machine)
        # Close the washing machine door
        achieve is_on(washing_machine)
        # Turn on the washing machine to start washing

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket for clothes
        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine) and plugged(washing_machine) and is_on(washing_machine)
        # Select the washing machine that is already plugged in and switched on

        if has_clothes_in_basket(basket):
            # If there are clothes in the basket, proceed to load them into the washing machine
            foreach clothes: item:
                if is_clothes(clothes) and inside(clothes, basket):
                    load_washing_machine(clothes, washing_machine)
            start_washing_machine(washing_machine)

#goal_representation_end

behavior load_clothes_into_washing_machine(c:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(c, washing_machine)

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve is_on(washing_machine)
        # Ensure the washing machine is turned on and stays on

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket for clothes

        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Select the washing machine

        foreach c: item:
            if is_clothes(c) and inside(c, basket):
                load_clothes_into_washing_machine(c, washing_machine)
                # Load each item of clothing into the washing machine

        start_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Start the washing machine to wash the clothes

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior load_clothes_into_washing_machine(c:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(c, washing_machine)
        # Place each piece of clothing inside the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once closed(washing_machine) # Close the washing machine door
        achieve is_on(washing_machine) # Turn on the washing machine

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket for clothes
        
        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine) and plugged(washing_machine) and is_on(washing_machine)
        # Select the washing machine that is already plugged and on
        
        foreach c: item:
            if is_clothes(c) and inside(c, basket):
                load_clothes_into_washing_machine(c, washing_machine)
        start_washing_machine(washing_machine) # Start the washing machine

#goal_representation_end

#goal_representation

behavior load_clothes(clothes:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(clothes, washing_machine)

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once closed(washing_machine)
        achieve_once is_on(washing_machine)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select basket for clothes

        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Select a washing machine

        foreach clothes: item:
            if is_clothes(clothes) and inside(clothes, basket):
                load_clothes(clothes, washing_machine)
        start_washing_machine(washing_machine) # Start the washing machine

#goal_representation_end

        achieve_once closed(washing_machine) # Close the washing machine door
        achieve is_on(washing_machine) # Ensure the washing machine is on

    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Select a basket for clothes and a washing machine
        foreach c: item:
            if is_clothes(c) and inside(c, basket):
                load_washing_machine(c, washing_machine)
                # Load each clothing item from the basket into the washing machine
        start_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Start the washing machine

    body:
        achieve_once inside(c, washing_machine)
        # Place the clothes inside the washing machine

    body:
        achieve is_on(washing_machine)
        # Ensure the washing machine is on

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the clothes basket
        
        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Select the washing machine

        foreach c: item:
        # Load all clothes from the basket into the washing machine
            if is_clothes(c) and inside(c, basket):
                load_clothes_into_washing_machine(c, washing_machine)

        # Start the washing machine

#goal_representation
behavior load_washing_machine(c:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(c, washing_machine)
        # Load clothes into the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once is_on(washing_machine)
        # Turn on the washing machine

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the clothes basket

        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine) and id[washing_machine]==2041
        # Select the washing machine with ID 2041

        foreach c: item:
        # Load all clothes from the basket into the washing machine
            if is_clothes(c) and inside(c, basket):
                load_washing_machine(c, washing_machine)
        
        start_washing_machine(washing_machine) # Start the washing machine
#goal_representation_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior load_washing_machine(clothing:item, machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(clothing, machine)
        # Place the clothing inside the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once closed(machine) # Close the washing machine door
        achieve is_on(machine) # Turn on the washing machine to start the cleaning process

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket for clothes

        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Select the washing machine

        foreach clothing: item:
            if is_clothes(clothing) and inside(clothing, basket):
                # Load all clothes from the basket into the washing machine
                load_washing_machine(clothing, washing_machine)

        start_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Start the washing machine to clean the clothes

#goal_representation_end

behavior load_clothes_into_washing_machine(c:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(c, washing_machine)
        # Place the clothing item inside the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once closed(washing_machine) # Ensure the washing machine door is closed
        achieve is_on(washing_machine) # Turn on the washing machine

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket for clothes
        
        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Select a washing machine

        foreach c: item:
        # Load all clothes from the basket into the washing machine
            if is_clothes(c) and inside(c, basket):
                load_clothes_into_washing_machine(c, washing_machine)
                
        start_washing_machine(washing_machine) # Start the washing machine

#goal_representation_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior load_clothes(clothes:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(clothes, washing_machine)
        # Load the clothes into the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once closed(washing_machine) # Ensure the washing machine door is closed
        achieve is_on(washing_machine) # Turn on the washing machine

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket for clothes
        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Select a washing machine
        foreach clothes: item:
        # Load all clothes from the basket into the washing machine
            if is_clothes(clothes) and inside(clothes, basket):
                load_clothes(clothes, washing_machine)
        start_washing_machine(washing_machine) # Start the washing machine

#goal_representation_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior load_clothes_into_washing_machine(c: item, washing_machine: item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(c, washing_machine)
        # Load the clothes into the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine: item):
    body:
        achieve_once is_on(washing_machine)
        # Turn on the washing machine to start washing clothes

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket for clothes

        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Select the washing machine
        
        foreach c: item:
            if is_clothes(c) and inside(c, basket):
                load_clothes_into_washing_machine(c, washing_machine)
        start_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Start the washing machine to wash the clothes

#goal_representation
 
behavior load_clothes_into_washing_machine(clothes:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(clothes, washing_machine)
        # Load each piece of clothing into the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once closed(washing_machine) # Close the washing machine door
        achieve_once is_on(washing_machine) # Turn on the washing machine

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select a basket for clothes
        
        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Select a washing machine

        foreach clothes: item:
        # Load all clothes from the basket into the washing machine
            if is_clothes(clothes) and dirty(clothes) and inside(clothes, basket):
                load_clothes_into_washing_machine(clothes, washing_machine)

        start_washing_machine(washing_machine) # Start the washing process

#goal_representation_end

behavior load_clothes(c:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(c, washing_machine)

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once closed(washing_machine) # Close the washing machine door
        achieve_once is_on(washing_machine) # Turn on the washing machine

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket for clothes

        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Select the washing machine

        foreach c: item:
            if is_clothes(c) and inside(c, basket):
                load_clothes(c, washing_machine)
        # Load all clothes from the basket into the washing machine

        start_washing_machine(washing_machine) # Start the washing machine

#goal_representation
 
behavior load_clothes_in_washing_machine(c:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(c, washing_machine)
        # Place the clothes inside the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once closed(washing_machine) # Close the washing machine door
        achieve is_on(washing_machine) # Ensure the washing machine is on

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Select the basket for clothes
        
        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine) and id[washing_machine]==2041
        # Select the washing machine with ID 2041
        
        foreach c: item:
        # Load all clothes from the basket into the washing machine
            if is_clothes(c) and inside(c, basket):
                load_clothes_in_washing_machine(c, washing_machine)
        
        start_washing_machine(washing_machine) # Start the washing machine

#goal_representation_end

behavior load_washing_machine(clothes:item, washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(clothes, washing_machine)
        # Place the clothes inside the washing machine

behavior start_washing_machine(washing_machine:item):
    body:
        achieve is_on(washing_machine)
        # Ensure the washing machine is turned on, starting the washing process

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind basket: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket)
        # Identifying the basket for clothes
        
        bind washing_machine: item where:
            is_washing_machine(washing_machine) and plugged(washing_machine)
        # Identifying the washing machine which is plugged in
        
        foreach clothes: item:
        # Place all clothes from the basket into the washing machine
            if is_clothes(clothes) and inside(clothes, basket):
                load_washing_machine(clothes, washing_machine)
        
        start_washing_machine(washing_machine)
        # Start the washing machine after loading all clothes
